The information about the device.

{\footnotesize\ttfamily -\/ ((deprecated(\char`\"{}deprecated, use) \mbox{\hyperlink{category_thing_smart_device_model_07_thing_smart_home_kit_08_a08003f7b44a6e97f47aa346c1dc3590d}{thingsdk\+\_\+associated\+Home\+Kit\+Device\+For\+Home\+Manager\+:}} \begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption}}

Find \mbox{\hyperlink{interface_thing_smart_home_kit_device}{Thing\+Smart\+Home\+Kit\+Device}} that associated with \mbox{\hyperlink{interface_thing_smart_device_model}{Thing\+Smart\+Device\+Model}} which has added in Home\+Kit. \begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
If The device has been added to Home\+Kit and is reachable, will return associated \mbox{\hyperlink{interface_thing_smart_home_kit_device}{Thing\+Smart\+Home\+Kit\+Device}}. If not found , will reutrn nil. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
When your device has been added to Home\+Kit, you can invoke {\ttfamily \mbox{[}\mbox{[}UIApplication shared\+Application\mbox{]} open\+URL\+:\mbox{[}NSURL URLWith\+String\+:@\char`\"{}com.\+apple.\+home\+://\char`\"{}\mbox{]} options\+:@\{\} completion\+Handler\+:nil\mbox{]};}, after user clicked the {\ttfamily Add To Home\+Kit} button in The Device Detail page. 
\end{DoxyNote}

\end{DoxyReturn}

\end{DoxyNote}
